 aisa anumaan he ki 15 june kii shaam se dilli samet uttar-pashchim bharat ke tamaam ilaakon main dhul kii maatra se garmi shuru ho jaaegi, aisa isliye hoga kyonki uttar pashchim bharat main aandhi pani kii activity bad jaaegi
 According to Meteorological Director Kuldeep Srivastava, dusty winds coming from Rajasthan are going up to two and a half kilometers above the surface of the ground
 in hawaaon kii raftaar 35 kilometre prati ghante tak ja rahi he
 Due to the anti-cyclonic circulation here, winds are coming from Rajasthan and approaching West Uttar Pradesh
 isaki vajah se dilli ensiaar ke upar dhul kii maatra zyada ikattha ho rahi he
 Kuldeep Srivastava says that this situation is not going to change in the next 24 hours, but from the evening of June 15, the speed of dusty winds coming from Rajasthan will decrease slightly, due to which all areas including delhi-ncr will come
 The amount of dust kept will reduce
 16 taarikh aate-aate uttarakhand or isse jude ilaakon main thunder storm kii activity shuru hone kaa anumaan he iskaa sidhaa asar uttar pashchim bharat main dhul bhari hawaaon par padegaa
 Hence it is expected that from 16th onwards, the havoc of dusty winds in Delhi, Punjab, Haryana, Western Uttar Pradesh will be reduced to a great extent
 dilli-ensiaar samet uttar bharat ke tamaam ilaakon main dhul bhari hawaaon ke aane kii vajah se PM 10 or PM 2
 The volume of 5 has reached alarming levels
 dilli main pichley 24 ghante main hawa main maujuud PM 10 kanon kii maatra saamaanya str ke mukaable ausatan 12 se 14 guna adhik he to vahiin PM 2
 Talking about the quantity of 5 particles, their volume is more than 4 times in the air compared to the normal level
 24 ghante main kam honge dhul ke kanayah aankade mausam vibhaag ke air quality forcast ke mutabik he
 According to the forecast, this quantity will decrease significantly in the next 24 hours, but even then the air condition will remain fierce at the pollution level
 is baar uttar bharat ke tamaam ilaakon main mausam kii sthitiyaan kaaphi ulat-pulat rahi hai, aise main dilli-ensiaar samet uttar-pashchim bharat ke tamaam ilaakon main monsoon se pehle vaataavaran main dhul kii baari maatra logon ko jarur chaukaa rahi he
 According to Meteorological Director Charan Singh, there is no need to be shocked, this type of weather in North West India is being seen because the monsoon is very weak at this time
 agle 7 dinon tak isamen dobaaraa takat aane kii sambhaavna nahin he is vajah se purvottar bharat main jhamajham barish ho rahi he
 At the same time, the process of heavy rains continues in the Western Ghats, but due to the weak monsoon, the thrust of the easterly winds from North India has completely ended
 is vajah se pachua hawaaon ne puure ilaake par apana raaj kaayam kar liya he
 In these conditions there is not much chance of relief from heat in North West India for next 7 days
 jab puraviya hawaaen kamjor ho gayi to unki jagah lene ke liye pachua hawaaen uttar bharat pahunchane lageen kyonki yah hawaaen rajasthan ke registan se hokar aa rahi thim or saath hi saath sataha par inaki raftaar kaaphi thi
 There was no scope of rain in Delhi, due to which it reached Delhi and surrounding areas with the sand of Rajasthan
 charan singh kaa kahana he ki agle 48 ghante main uttarakhand or himalay kii talahati vaale ilaakon main aandhi pani kii activity shuru ho jaaegi
 Due to this, there is also possibility of cloud movement in delhi-ncr on June 17 but there is still no scope of rain in Delhi
 mausamake jaankaron kaa kahana he ki agle 7 dinon main monsoon ek baar phir se jor pakadega uske baad hi uttar pashchim bharat main mausam kaa rukh badalata hua najar aayega
